2. DriverFactory.java — ThreadLocal Browser Management

package utils;

import io.github.bonigarcia.wdm.WebDriverManager;
import org.openqa.selenium.WebDriver;
import org.openqa.selenium.chrome.ChromeDriver;
import org.openqa.selenium.chrome.ChromeOptions;
import org.openqa.selenium.firefox.FirefoxDriver;
import org.openqa.selenium.edge.EdgeDriver;

public class DriverFactory {

    private static final ThreadLocal<WebDriver> driverThread = new ThreadLocal<>();

    public static WebDriver getDriver() {
        if (driverThread.get() == null) {
            driverThread.set(createDriver());
        }
        return driverThread.get();
    }

    private static WebDriver createDriver() {
        String browser = System.getProperty("browser", "chrome").toLowerCase();
        boolean headless = Boolean.parseBoolean(
            System.getProperty("headless", "false"));

        return switch (browser) {
            case "firefox" -> {
                WebDriverManager.firefoxdriver().setup();
                yield new FirefoxDriver();
            }
            case "edge" -> {
                WebDriverManager.edgedriver().setup();
                yield new EdgeDriver();
            }
            default -> {
                WebDriverManager.chromedriver().setup();
                ChromeOptions options = new ChromeOptions();
                if (headless) options.addArguments("--headless=new");
                options.addArguments("--disable-gpu", "--no-sandbox");
                yield new ChromeDriver(options);
            }
        };
    }

    public static void quitDriver() {
        if (driverThread.get() != null) {
            driverThread.get().quit();
            driverThread.remove();
        }
    }
}

3. ConfigReader.java

package utils;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.util.Properties;

public class ConfigReader {

    private static Properties properties = new Properties();

    public static void load(String env) {
        String file = "config/" + env + ".properties";
        try (InputStream input = ConfigReader.class
                .getClassLoader().getResourceAsStream(file)) {
            if (input == null) {
                throw new RuntimeException("Config file not found: " + file);
            }
            properties.load(input);
        } catch (IOException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to load config: " + file, e);
        }
    }

    public static String get(String key) {
        String sysVal = System.getProperty(key);
        return sysVal != null ? sysVal : properties.getProperty(key);
    }
}

4. BasePage.java — Common Page Methods

package pages;

import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.PageFactory;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.ExpectedConditions;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.WebDriverWait;
import utils.DriverFactory;
import java.time.Duration;

public abstract class BasePage {

    protected WebDriver driver;
    protected WebDriverWait wait;

    public BasePage() {
        this.driver = DriverFactory.getDriver();
        this.wait = new WebDriverWait(driver, Duration.ofSeconds(15));
        PageFactory.initElements(driver, this);
    }

    protected void click(WebElement element) {
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.elementToBeClickable(element)).click();
    }

    protected void type(WebElement element, String text) {
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOf(element));
        element.clear();
        element.sendKeys(text);
    }

    protected String getText(WebElement element) {
        return wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOf(element)).getText();
    }

    protected boolean isDisplayed(WebElement element) {
        try {
            return wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOf(element)).isDisplayed();
        } catch (TimeoutException e) {
            return false;
        }
    }
}

5. LoginPage.java — Page Object with PageFactory

package pages;

import org.openqa.selenium.WebElement;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.FindBy;

public class LoginPage extends BasePage {

    @FindBy(id = "username")
    private WebElement usernameField;

    @FindBy(id = "password")
    private WebElement passwordField;

    @FindBy(id = "login-btn")
    private WebElement loginButton;

    @FindBy(css = ".error-message")
    private WebElement errorMessage;

    public void enterUsername(String username) { type(usernameField, username); }
    public void enterPassword(String password) { type(passwordField, password); }
    public void clickLogin() { click(loginButton); }

    public void login(String username, String password) {
        enterUsername(username);
        enterPassword(password);
        clickLogin();
    }

    public String getErrorMessage() { return getText(errorMessage); }
    public boolean isLoginPageDisplayed() { return isDisplayed(usernameField); }

    public void navigateToLogin() {
        driver.get(utils.ConfigReader.get("base.url") + "/login");
    }
}

6. login.feature — Three Scenarios

@login
Feature: User Login
  As a registered user
  I want to login to the application
  So that I can access my account

  Background:
    Given I navigate to the login page

  @smoke @positive
  Scenario: Successful login with valid credentials
    When I enter username "testuser" and password "pass123"
    And I click the login button
    Then I should be redirected to the home page
    And the welcome message should contain "Welcome, testuser"

  @negative
  Scenario: Login fails with invalid password
    When I enter username "testuser" and password "wrongpass"
    And I click the login button
    Then I should see an error message "Invalid username or password"
    And I should remain on the login page

  @negative
  Scenario Outline: Login fails with empty fields
    When I enter username "<username>" and password "<password>"
    And I click the login button
    Then I should see an error message "<error>"

    Examples:
      | username  | password  | error                |
      |           | pass123   | Username is required |
      | testuser  |           | Password is required |
      |           |           | All fields required  |

7. LoginSteps.java

package stepdefinitions;

import context.TestContext;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.testng.Assert;
import pages.HomePage;
import pages.LoginPage;

public class LoginSteps {

    private TestContext testContext;
    private LoginPage loginPage;
    private HomePage homePage;

    public LoginSteps(TestContext testContext) {
        this.testContext = testContext;
        this.loginPage = new LoginPage();
        this.homePage = new HomePage();
    }

    @Given("I navigate to the login page")
    public void navigateToLoginPage() {
        loginPage.navigateToLogin();
        Assert.assertTrue(loginPage.isLoginPageDisplayed());
    }

    @When("I enter username {string} and password {string}")
    public void enterCredentials(String username, String password) {
        loginPage.enterUsername(username);
        loginPage.enterPassword(password);
        testContext.setUsername(username);
    }

    @When("I click the login button")
    public void clickLoginButton() { loginPage.clickLogin(); }

    @Then("I should be redirected to the home page")
    public void verifyHomePage() {
        Assert.assertTrue(homePage.isHomePageDisplayed());
    }

    @Then("the welcome message should contain {string}")
    public void verifyWelcomeMessage(String expected) {
        Assert.assertTrue(homePage.getWelcomeMessage().contains(expected));
    }

    @Then("I should see an error message {string}")
    public void verifyErrorMessage(String expected) {
        Assert.assertEquals(loginPage.getErrorMessage(), expected);
    }

    @Then("I should remain on the login page")
    public void verifyOnLoginPage() {
        Assert.assertTrue(loginPage.isLoginPageDisplayed());
    }
}

8. Hooks.java — Browser, Screenshot, Cleanup

package hooks;

import context.TestContext;
import io.cucumber.java.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import utils.ConfigReader;
import utils.DriverFactory;

public class Hooks {

    private static final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(Hooks.class);
    private WebDriver driver;
    private TestContext testContext;

    public Hooks(TestContext testContext) { this.testContext = testContext; }

    @BeforeAll
    public static void beforeAll() {
        ConfigReader.load(System.getProperty("env", "qa"));
    }

    @Before
    public void setUp(Scenario scenario) {
        driver = DriverFactory.getDriver();
        driver.manage().window().maximize();
        driver.get(ConfigReader.get("base.url"));
        logger.info("Started: {}", scenario.getName());
    }

    @After
    public void tearDown(Scenario scenario) {
        if (scenario.isFailed()) {
            byte[] screenshot = ((TakesScreenshot) driver)
                .getScreenshotAs(OutputType.BYTES);
            scenario.attach(screenshot, "image/png", "Failure Screenshot");
        }
        testContext.clear();
        DriverFactory.quitDriver();
    }
}

9. TestContext.java — Sharing State Between Steps

package context;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public class TestContext {

    private final Map<String, Object> context = new HashMap<>();
    private String username;

    public void set(String key, Object value) { context.put(key, value); }
    public Object get(String key) { return context.get(key); }
    public void setUsername(String username) {
        this.username = username;
        context.put("username", username);
    }
    public String getUsername() { return username; }
    public void clear() { context.clear(); username = null; }
}

10. SmokeRunner.java

package runners;

import io.cucumber.testng.AbstractTestNGCucumberTests;
import io.cucumber.testng.CucumberOptions;
import org.testng.annotations.DataProvider;

@CucumberOptions(
    features = "src/test/resources/features",
    glue = {"stepdefinitions", "hooks", "context"},
    plugin = {
        "pretty",
        "html:target/cucumber-report.html",
        "json:target/cucumber.json",
        "io.qameta.allure.cucumber7jvm.AllureCucumber7Jvm"
    },
    tags = "@smoke"
)
public class SmokeRunner extends AbstractTestNGCucumberTests {

    @Override
    @DataProvider(parallel = true)
    public Object[][] scenarios() { return super.scenarios(); }
}

11. testng.xml

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE suite SYSTEM "https://testng.org/testng-1.0.dtd">
<suite name="BDD Automation Suite" parallel="methods" thread-count="3">

    <listeners>
        <listener class-name="io.qameta.allure.testng.AllureTestNg"/>
    </listeners>

    <test name="Smoke Tests">
        <classes><class name="runners.SmokeRunner"/></classes>
    </test>

    <test name="Regression Tests">
        <classes><class name="runners.RegressionRunner"/></classes>
    </test>
</suite>

Framework Design Patterns Used

PatternWhere AppliedBenefit
Page Object Model (POM)pages/ packageEncapsulates locators and actions; single place to update UI changes
Factory PatternDriverFactory.javaCreates browser instances based on config; hides creation logic
ThreadLocal PatternDriverFactory ThreadLocalThread-safe driver for parallel scenario execution
Dependency InjectionCucumber PicoContainerShares TestContext across step definition classes
Singleton (Config)ConfigReader static PropertiesSingle config load per JVM run
Strategy PatternBrowser selection in DriverFactorySwitch browser at runtime via -Dbrowser
Facade PatternBasePage common methodsSimplifies wait/click/type for all page objects
BDD / Layered Architecturefeatures → steps → pages → utilsSeparates business language from technical implementation

Interview Q&A — Full BDD Framework

#QuestionAnswer
1Describe your BDD framework architecture.Feature files → Step Definitions → Page Objects → Utilities; TestNG for parallel execution; Cucumber hooks for setup/teardown.
2Why use ThreadLocal for WebDriver?Each parallel scenario thread needs its own driver instance to avoid cross-test interference.
3How do you share data between step definition classes?TestContext injected via Cucumber PicoContainer constructor injection.
4What is the role of BasePage?Abstract parent providing common wait, click, type methods using WebDriverWait and PageFactory.
5How do you run smoke vs regression?Separate runner classes with different tags referenced in testng.xml test blocks.
6How to switch environments?-Denv=qa loads the corresponding properties file in ConfigReader via @BeforeAll hook.
7Where do you capture screenshots?Hooks @After — scenario.attach() on failure; embedded in Allure/Cucumber HTML reports.
8Why PageFactory over direct findElement?Lazy initialization of @FindBy elements; cleaner page classes.
9How to handle test data?Scenario Outline Examples tables, Excel via ExcelReader, or config properties.
10How is the framework CI-ready?Maven + testng.xml + system properties + JSON/Allure report artifacts.
11What goes in main vs test source?main/java: pages, utils, context; test/java: runners, steps, hooks, features.
12How to avoid duplicate step definitions?One step class per feature domain; reuse via common step classes in glue path.

Section 28: API Testing with Cucumber

REST Assured + Cucumber Integration

API testing in a BDD framework uses REST Assured for HTTP calls and Cucumber for readable Gherkin scenarios. The same hooks, reporting, and CI pipeline as UI tests apply — only the step definitions change from Selenium to REST Assured.

Architecture: Feature files describe API behavior in business language. Step definitions build requests, send them via REST Assured, and assert responses using Hamcrest matchers or JSONPath.

Dependencies

<dependency>
    <groupId>io.rest-assured</groupId>
    <artifactId>rest-assured</artifactId>
    <version>5.4.0</version>
</dependency>
<dependency>
    <groupId>io.rest-assured</groupId>
    <artifactId>json-path</artifactId>
    <version>5.4.0</version>
</dependency>
<dependency>
    <groupId>mysql</groupId>
    <artifactId>mysql-connector-java</artifactId>
    <version>8.0.33</version>
</dependency>

Feature File for API Testing

@api
Feature: User API
  As an API consumer
  I want to manage users via REST endpoints
  So that I can verify backend behavior

  @smoke
  Scenario: Create user via API
    Given the API base URL is "https://api.example.com"
    When I send a POST request to "/users" with body:
      | name  | email           |
      | QA    | qa@example.com  |
    Then the response status code should be 201
    And the response body should contain "id"
    And the response JSON path "$.email" should be "qa@example.com"

  Scenario: Get user by ID
    Given the API base URL is "https://api.example.com"
    And a user exists with id "1"
    When I send a GET request to "/users/1"
    Then the response status code should be 200
    And the response JSON path "$.name" should be "QA"

  @negative
  Scenario: Create user with invalid email returns 400
    Given the API base URL is "https://api.example.com"
    When I send a POST request to "/users" with body:
      | name  | email       |
      | QA    | invalid     |
    Then the response status code should be 400
    And the response body should contain "Invalid email"

Complete APISteps.java with REST Assured

package stepdefinitions;

import context.TestContext;
import io.cucumber.datatable.DataTable;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import io.restassured.response.Response;
import io.restassured.specification.RequestSpecification;
import org.testng.Assert;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

import static io.restassured.RestAssured.*;
import static org.hamcrest.Matchers.*;

public class APISteps {

    private TestContext testContext;
    private RequestSpecification request;
    private Response response;

    public APISteps(TestContext testContext) {
        this.testContext = testContext;
    }

    @Given("the API base URL is {string}")
    public void setBaseUrl(String baseUrl) {
        baseURI = baseUrl;
        request = given()
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .header("Accept", "application/json");
    }

    @Given("a user exists with id {string}")
    public void userExists(String id) {
        testContext.set("userId", id);
    }

    @When("I send a GET request to {string}")
    public void sendGetRequest(String endpoint) {
        response = request.when().get(endpoint);
        testContext.set("response", response);
    }

    @When("I send a POST request to {string} with body:")
    public void sendPostRequest(String endpoint, DataTable dataTable) {
        Map<String, String> body = dataTable.asMaps().get(0);
        response = request
            .body(body)
            .when()
            .post(endpoint);
        testContext.set("response", response);
        testContext.set("requestBody", body);
    }

    @When("I send a PUT request to {string} with body:")
    public void sendPutRequest(String endpoint, DataTable dataTable) {
        Map<String, String> body = dataTable.asMaps().get(0);
        response = request.body(body).when().put(endpoint);
        testContext.set("response", response);
    }

    @When("I send a DELETE request to {string}")
    public void sendDeleteRequest(String endpoint) {
        response = request.when().delete(endpoint);
        testContext.set("response", response);
    }

    @Then("the response status code should be {int}")
    public void verifyStatusCode(int expectedStatus) {
        response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        Assert.assertEquals(response.getStatusCode(), expectedStatus,
            "Status code mismatch. Body: " + response.getBody().asString());
    }

    @Then("the response body should contain {string}")
    public void verifyBodyContains(String expectedText) {
        response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        Assert.assertTrue(response.getBody().asString().contains(expectedText),
            "Response body does not contain: " + expectedText);
    }

    @Then("the response JSON path {string} should be {string}")
    public void verifyJsonPath(String jsonPath, String expectedValue) {
        response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        String actual = response.jsonPath().getString(jsonPath);
        Assert.assertEquals(actual, expectedValue,
            "JSONPath " + jsonPath + " mismatch");
    }

    @Then("the response header {string} should be {string}")
    public void verifyHeader(String headerName, String expectedValue) {
        response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        Assert.assertEquals(response.getHeader(headerName), expectedValue);
    }

    @Then("the response time should be less than {int} ms")
    public void verifyResponseTime(int maxMs) {
        response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        Assert.assertTrue(response.getTime() < maxMs,
            "Response time " + response.getTime() + "ms exceeded " + maxMs + "ms");
    }
}

JSON Body from Data Tables

Cucumber Data Tables map naturally to JSON request bodies. For nested JSON, convert the table to a Map or use a JSON template:

@When("I send a POST request to {string} with JSON body:")
public void sendPostWithJson(String endpoint, String jsonBody) {
    response = request.body(jsonBody).when().post(endpoint);
    testContext.set("response", response);
}

// Feature file usage with doc string:
// When I send a POST request to "/orders" with JSON body:
//   """
//   {"productId": 101, "quantity": 2, "shipping": {"city": "NYC"}}
//   """

JSONPath Assertions

// Hamcrest fluent validation (alternative approach)
response.then()
    .statusCode(201)
    .body("id", notNullValue())
    .body("email", equalTo("qa@example.com"))
    .body("orders.size()", greaterThan(0))
    .body("orders[0].productId", equalTo(101));

// Extract values for DB validation
int userId = response.jsonPath().getInt("id");
testContext.set("createdUserId", userId);

API + DB Validation in BDD

Combine API response validation with database record verification for end-to-end backend testing.

  Scenario: Create user and verify in database
    Given the API base URL is "https://api.example.com"
    And the database connection is established
    When I send a POST request to "/users" with body:
      | name     | email              |
      | DBTest   | dbtest@example.com |
    Then the response status code should be 201
    And the user "dbtest@example.com" should exist in the database
    And the database user count should be greater than 0

JDBC Step Definitions

package stepdefinitions;

import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.testng.Assert;
import utils.DatabaseHelper;

public class DatabaseSteps {

    private DatabaseHelper dbHelper;

    public DatabaseSteps() {
        this.dbHelper = new DatabaseHelper();
    }

    @Given("the database connection is established")
    public void connectDatabase() {
        dbHelper.connect();
    }

    @Then("the user {string} should exist in the database")
    public void verifyUserInDb(String email) {
        int count = dbHelper.queryForInt(
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE email = ?", email);
        Assert.assertEquals(count, 1, "User not found in database: " + email);
    }

    @Then("the database user count should be greater than {int}")
    public void verifyUserCount(int minCount) {
        int count = dbHelper.queryForInt("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users");
        Assert.assertTrue(count > minCount);
    }

    @Then("I delete the test user {string} from the database")
    public void deleteTestUser(String email) {
        dbHelper.execute("DELETE FROM users WHERE email = ?", email);
    }
}

API Test Framework Structure

api-bdd-framework/
├── src/test/java/
│   ├── runners/

Complete Runner for API Tests

package runners;

import io.cucumber.testng.AbstractTestNGCucumberTests;
import io.cucumber.testng.CucumberOptions;
import org.testng.annotations.DataProvider;

@CucumberOptions(
    features = "src/test/resources/features",
    glue = {"stepdefinitions", "hooks", "context"},
    plugin = {
        "pretty",
        "html:target/api-report.html",
        "json:target/api-cucumber.json",
        "io.qameta.allure.cucumber7jvm.AllureCucumber7Jvm"
    },
    tags = "@api"
)
public class APIRunner extends AbstractTestNGCucumberTests {

    @Override
    @DataProvider(parallel = true)
    public Object[][] scenarios() {
        return super.scenarios();
    }
}

API Hooks (No Browser)

@Before("@api")
public void setUpApi() {
    RestAssured.enableLoggingOfRequestAndResponseIfValidationFails();
}

@After("@api")
public void tearDownApi(Scenario scenario) {
    if (scenario.isFailed()) {
        Response response = (Response) testContext.get("response");
        if (response != null) {
            scenario.attach(response.getBody().asString(),
                "application/json", "API Response Body");
        }
    }
}

Interview Q&A — API Testing with Cucumber

#QuestionAnswer
1How do you integrate REST Assured with Cucumber?Create step definitions that use REST Assured given/when/then DSL; store Response in TestContext for cross-step assertions.
2How to pass JSON body from feature file?Use Data Tables with asMaps() for flat JSON, or doc strings (""") for nested JSON bodies.
3How to validate JSON response fields?response.jsonPath().getString("$.field") with Assert, or Hamcrest matchers via response.then().body().
4Can UI and API tests share the same framework?Yes — separate feature files and step classes; tag @ui vs @api; conditional hooks skip browser for API tests.
5How to validate API response AND database?Assert response in API steps; use JDBC steps to query DB and verify record exists with matching fields.
6How to handle authentication in API steps?Set auth token in @Before("@api") hook or Given step: request.header("Authorization", "Bearer " + token).
7How to chain API calls in one scenario?Store response values (e.g., created user ID) in TestContext; subsequent steps read from context.
8How to test response time in BDD?Step: "the response time should be less than 500 ms" — assert response.getTime() < maxMs.
9How to attach API response to report on failure?In @After hook, scenario.attach(response.getBody().asString(), "application/json", "Response").
10REST Assured vs HttpClient in Cucumber?REST Assured provides fluent DSL, built-in JSONPath, Hamcrest integration — ideal for BDD readability.
11How to parameterize API base URL?Given step accepts URL string, or read from ConfigReader based on -Denv system property.
12How to run only API tests in CI?mvn test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@api" with APIRunner in testng.xml.

Section 29: Jenkins + Cucumber/TestNG Integration

CI/CD Pipeline for BDD Framework

Jenkins orchestrates the full BDD test lifecycle — from code checkout through Maven build, parallel TestNG/Cucumber execution, report generation, and stakeholder notification.

Pipeline Architecture

┌──────────┐    ┌──────────┐    ┌──────────┐    ┌──────────┐
│   Git    │───→│ Jenkins  │───→│  Maven   │───→│  TestNG  │
│  (Push/  │    │ Pipeline │    │  Build   │    │  Runner  │
│   PR)    │    │          │    │          │    │          │
└──────────┘    └──────────┘    └──────────┘    └────┬─────┘
                                                      │
                                                      ▼
                                               ┌──────────┐
                                               │ Cucumber │
                                               │ Scenarios│
                                               │(Parallel)│
                                               └────┬─────┘
                                                    │
                    ┌───────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────┐
                    ▼                               ▼                               ▼
             ┌────────────┐                 ┌────────────┐                 ┌────────────┐
             │  Cucumber  │                 │   Allure   │                 │   Email /  │
             │ JSON/HTML  │                 │   Report   │                 │   Slack    │
             │  Reports   │                 │  Dashboard │                 │ Notification│
             └────────────┘                 └────────────┘                 └────────────┘

Complete Jenkinsfile

pipeline {
    agent any

    parameters {
        choice(name: 'TAG', choices: ['@smoke', '@regression', '@full'],
               description: 'Cucumber tag to execute')
        choice(name: 'ENV', choices: ['qa', 'staging'],
               description: 'Target environment')
        choice(name: 'BROWSER', choices: ['chrome', 'firefox', 'edge'],
               description: 'Browser for UI tests')
        booleanParam(name: 'HEADLESS', defaultValue: true,
                     description: 'Run browser in headless mode')
    }

    environment {
        MAVEN_OPTS = '-Xmx1024m'
        ALLURE_RESULTS = 'target/allure-results'
    }

    stages {
        stage('Checkout') {
            steps {
                checkout scm
            }
        }

        stage('Build') {
            steps {
                sh 'mvn clean compile -B'
            }
        }

        stage('Smoke Tests') {
            when { expression { params.TAG == '@smoke' || params.TAG == '@full' } }
            steps {
                sh """
                    mvn test -B \
                      -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@smoke" \
                      -Denv=${params.ENV} \
                      -Dbrowser=${params.BROWSER} \
                      -Dheadless=${params.HEADLESS}
                """
            }
            post {
                always {
                    cucumber fileIncludePattern: 'target/cucumber.json'
                    archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'target/cucumber-report.html', allowEmptyArchive: true
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Regression Tests') {
            when { expression { params.TAG == '@regression' || params.TAG == '@full' } }
            parallel {
                stage('Regression - Chrome') {
                    steps {
                        sh """
                            mvn test -B \
                              -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@regression" \
                              -Denv=${params.ENV} \
                              -Dbrowser=chrome \
                              -Dheadless=true
                        """
                    }
                }
                stage('Regression - Firefox') {
                    steps {
                        sh """
                            mvn test -B \
                              -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@regression" \
                              -Denv=${params.ENV} \
                              -Dbrowser=firefox \
                              -Dheadless=true
                        """
                    }
                }
            }
            post {
                always {
                    cucumber fileIncludePattern: 'target/cucumber.json'
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Allure Report') {
            steps {
                allure includeProperties: false,
                       jdk: '',
                       results: [[path: "${ALLURE_RESULTS}"]]
            }
        }
    }

    post {
        always {
            junit 'target/cucumber-junit.xml'
            archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'target/**/*-report*, target/allure-results/**',
                             allowEmptyArchive: true
        }
        success {
            emailext(
                subject: "✔ BDD Tests PASSED - ${env.JOB_NAME} #${env.BUILD_NUMBER}",
                body: """Build ${env.BUILD_URL} succeeded.
                         Environment: ${params.ENV} | Tag: ${params.TAG}
                         Allure Report: ${env.BUILD_URL}allure""",
                to: '${DEFAULT_RECIPIENTS}'
            )
        }
        failure {
            emailext(
                subject: "✘ BDD Tests FAILED - ${env.JOB_NAME} #${env.BUILD_NUMBER}",
                body: """Build ${env.BUILD_URL} failed.
                         Check console output and Allure report.""",
                to: '${DEFAULT_RECIPIENTS}'
            )
        }
    }
}

Jenkins Parameterized Build

ParameterOptionsPurpose
TAG@smoke, @regression, @fullSelect which test suite to execute
ENVqa, stagingTarget environment — loads corresponding config properties
BROWSERchrome, firefox, edgeBrowser selection passed to DriverFactory
HEADLESStrue / falseHeadless mode for CI agents without display

Maven Command in Jenkins

# Smoke tests on QA with Chrome
mvn clean test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@smoke" -Dbrowser=chrome -Denv=qa

# Regression with parallel threads
mvn clean test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@regression" -Dbrowser=chrome -Denv=staging -Dheadless=true

# API tests only
mvn clean test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@api" -Denv=qa

# Full suite with Allure
mvn clean test -Denv=qa -Dbrowser=chrome
allure generate target/allure-results -o target/allure-report

Cucumber JSON Report in Jenkins

Install the Cucumber Reports Plugin in Jenkins. After test execution, publish results:

post {
    always {
        cucumber fileIncludePattern: '**/cucumber.json'
        archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'target/cucumber-report.html'
    }
}

This renders feature/scenario pass-fail trends directly in the Jenkins build page with drill-down to failed steps.

Allure Report in Jenkins

Install the Allure Plugin. Configure the pipeline stage:

stage('Allure Report') {
    steps {
        allure includeProperties: false,
               results: [[path: 'target/allure-results']]
    }
}

Allure dashboard appears as a sidebar link on each build with history, severity, and screenshot attachments.

Scheduled Execution (Nightly Regression)

triggers {
    cron('H 2 * * 1-5')  // Nightly at ~2 AM, Mon-Fri
}

// Or in Jenkins job config:
// Build Triggers → Build periodically → H 2 * * *
// Maven goal: clean test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@regression" -Denv=qa -Dheadless=true

Slack / Teams Notification

post {
    always {
        script {
            def status = currentBuild.currentResult
            def color  = status == 'SUCCESS' ? 'good' : 'danger'
            def emoji  = status == 'SUCCESS' ? '✔' : '✘'

            slackSend(
                channel: '#qa-automation',
                color: color,
                message: "${emoji} *${env.JOB_NAME}* #${env.BUILD_NUMBER} - ${status}\n" +
                         "Tag: ${params.TAG} | Env: ${params.ENV} | Browser: ${params.BROWSER}\n" +
                         "<${env.BUILD_URL}|View Build> | <${env.BUILD_URL}allure|Allure Report>"
            )
        }
    }
}
Microsoft Teams: Use the Office 365 Connector plugin or webhook notification step with Adaptive Card JSON containing build status, report links, and failure summary.

Jenkins Pipeline Best Practices for BDD

  • Archive reports always — use post { always { } } so reports are saved even on failure.
  • Parameterize everything — tag, env, browser — avoid hardcoding in Jenkinsfile.
  • Run smoke on every commit — gate merges with fast @smoke suite (< 10 min).
  • Parallel regression — split by browser or feature tag in parallel stages.
  • Headless by default — CI agents rarely have a display; pass -Dheadless=true.
  • Separate API and UI stages — API tests run faster without browser overhead.
  • Pin Maven/ JDK versions — use Jenkins tools directive for reproducible builds.

Interview Q&A — Jenkins + Cucumber/TestNG

#QuestionAnswer
1How do you integrate Cucumber tests with Jenkins?Jenkinsfile runs mvn test with Cucumber runner; publish cucumber.json via Cucumber Reports plugin; archive HTML/Allure artifacts.
2How to select Cucumber tags in Jenkins?Parameterized build with TAG choice parameter passed as -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@smoke".
3How to run smoke and regression in parallel?Use parallel { stage('Smoke') {} stage('Regression') {} } in declarative pipeline.
4What Maven command runs BDD tests?mvn clean test -Dcucumber.filter.tags="@smoke" -Dbrowser=chrome -Denv=qa
5How to publish Cucumber reports in Jenkins?Install Cucumber Reports plugin; add cucumber fileIncludePattern: 'target/cucumber.json' in post block.
6How to generate Allure report in Jenkins?Install Allure plugin; add allure results stage pointing to target/allure-results.
7How to schedule nightly regression?cron('H 2 * * 1-5') trigger in Jenkinsfile or periodic build trigger in job config.
8How to notify team on test failure?post { failure { emailext / slackSend } } with build URL and Allure report link.
9How to switch environments in CI?Parameterized ENV choice passed as -Denv=qa; ConfigReader loads matching properties file.
10How to handle test artifacts?archiveArtifacts for HTML reports, screenshots, cucumber.json, allure-results in post always block.
11Should smoke tests gate deployments?Yes — run @smoke on every PR/commit; fail the pipeline if smoke fails to prevent broken deploys.
12How to run tests headless in Jenkins?Pass -Dheadless=true system property; DriverFactory reads it and adds --headless Chrome argument.

Section 30: Real-Time Project Scenarios

Scenario 1: Login Automation

Requirement

Automate login for a web application supporting three authentication methods: email/password, SSO (OAuth redirect), and OTP (one-time password). Tests must run via TestNG + Cucumber, use Page Object Model, and validate success/failure states with screenshots on failure.

Feature File (Gherkin)

Feature: User Login
  As a registered user
  I want to log in using multiple methods
  So that I can access the application securely

  Background:
    Given the login page is open

  @smoke @email
  Scenario: Successful login with valid email credentials
    When I login with email "user@test.com" and password "Pass@123"
    Then I should see the dashboard with welcome message "Welcome, User"

  @negative
  Scenario: Failed login with invalid password
    When I login with email "user@test.com" and password "WrongPass"
    Then I should see error message "Invalid credentials"

  @negative
  Scenario: Failed login with empty email
    When I login with email "" and password "Pass@123"
    Then I should see error message "Email is required"

  @sso
  Scenario: Successful SSO login via Google
    When I click SSO button "Google"
    And I complete SSO authentication with provider "google"
    Then I should be redirected to dashboard

  @sso @negative
  Scenario: SSO login cancelled by user
    When I click SSO button "Google"
    And I cancel SSO authentication
    Then I should remain on login page
    And I should see message "Authentication cancelled"

  @otp
  Scenario: Successful OTP login
    When I request OTP for mobile "9876543210"
    And I enter OTP "123456"
    Then I should see the dashboard

  @otp @negative
  Scenario: Failed OTP login with expired code
    When I request OTP for mobile "9876543210"
    And I enter OTP "000000"
    Then I should see error message "Invalid or expired OTP"

Step Definition (Java)

package com.automation.steps;

import com.automation.pages.LoginPage;
import com.automation.pages.DashboardPage;
import com.automation.utils.DriverFactory;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.WebDriver;
import org.testng.Assert;

public class LoginSteps {
    private WebDriver driver;
    private LoginPage loginPage;
    private DashboardPage dashboardPage;

    @Given("the login page is open")
    public void openLoginPage() {
        driver = DriverFactory.getDriver();
        driver.get("https://app.example.com/login");
        loginPage = new LoginPage(driver);
    }

    @When("I login with email {string} and password {string}")
    public void loginWithEmail(String email, String password) {
        loginPage.enterEmail(email);
        loginPage.enterPassword(password);
        loginPage.clickLoginButton();
    }

    @When("I click SSO button {string}")
    public void clickSSO(String provider) {
        loginPage.clickSSOProvider(provider);
    }

    @When("I complete SSO authentication with provider {string}")
    public void completeSSO(String provider) {
        loginPage.handleSSOPopup(provider, "sso-user@test.com", "SSOPass@123");
    }

    @When("I cancel SSO authentication")
    public void cancelSSO() {
        loginPage.cancelSSOPopup();
    }

    @When("I request OTP for mobile {string}")
    public void requestOTP(String mobile) {
        loginPage.switchToOTPTab();
        loginPage.enterMobile(mobile);
        loginPage.clickSendOTP();
    }

    @When("I enter OTP {string}")
    public void enterOTP(String otp) {
        loginPage.enterOTP(otp);
        loginPage.clickVerifyOTP();
    }

    @Then("I should see the dashboard with welcome message {string}")
    public void verifyDashboardWelcome(String message) {
        dashboardPage = new DashboardPage(driver);
        Assert.assertTrue(dashboardPage.isDisplayed());
        Assert.assertEquals(dashboardPage.getWelcomeMessage(), message);
    }

    @Then("I should see the dashboard")
    public void verifyDashboard() {
        dashboardPage = new DashboardPage(driver);
        Assert.assertTrue(dashboardPage.isDisplayed());
    }

    @Then("I should see error message {string}")
    public void verifyError(String expected) {
        Assert.assertEquals(loginPage.getErrorMessage(), expected);
    }

    @Then("I should be redirected to dashboard")
    public void verifyRedirect() {
        Assert.assertTrue(driver.getCurrentUrl().contains("/dashboard"));
    }

    @Then("I should remain on login page")
    public void verifyOnLoginPage() {
        Assert.assertTrue(driver.getCurrentUrl().contains("/login"));
    }

    @Then("I should see message {string}")
    public void verifyMessage(String msg) {
        Assert.assertEquals(loginPage.getInfoMessage(), msg);
    }
}

Page Object

package com.automation.pages;

import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.*;

public class LoginPage {
    private WebDriver driver;
    private WebDriverWait wait;

    private By emailField    = By.id("email");
    private By passwordField = By.id("password");
    private By loginBtn      = By.cssSelector("button[type='submit']");
    private By errorMsg      = By.cssSelector(".error-message");
    private By infoMsg       = By.cssSelector(".info-message");
    private By otpTab        = By.id("otp-tab");
    private By mobileField   = By.id("mobile");
    private By sendOtpBtn    = By.id("send-otp");
    private By otpField      = By.id("otp-input");
    private By verifyOtpBtn  = By.id("verify-otp");

    public LoginPage(WebDriver driver) {
        this.driver = driver;
        this.wait = new WebDriverWait(driver, Duration.ofSeconds(15));
    }

    public void enterEmail(String email) {
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(emailField));
        driver.findElement(emailField).clear();
        driver.findElement(emailField).sendKeys(email);
    }

    public void enterPassword(String password) {
        driver.findElement(passwordField).clear();
        driver.findElement(passwordField).sendKeys(password);
    }

    public void clickLoginButton() {
        driver.findElement(loginBtn).click();
    }

    public void clickSSOProvider(String provider) {
        driver.findElement(By.cssSelector("[data-provider='" + provider.toLowerCase() + "']")).click();
    }

    public void handleSSOPopup(String provider, String user, String pass) {
        String mainWindow = driver.getWindowHandle();
        wait.until(d -> d.getWindowHandles().size() > 1);
        for (String handle : driver.getWindowHandles()) {
            if (!handle.equals(mainWindow)) {
                driver.switchTo().window(handle);
                break;
            }
        }
        driver.findElement(By.id("identifierId")).sendKeys(user);
        driver.findElement(By.id("identifierNext")).click();
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(By.name("Passwd")));
        driver.findElement(By.name("Passwd")).sendKeys(pass);
        driver.findElement(By.id("passwordNext")).click();
        driver.switchTo().window(mainWindow);
    }

    public void cancelSSOPopup() {
        String mainWindow = driver.getWindowHandle();
        wait.until(d -> d.getWindowHandles().size() > 1);
        for (String handle : driver.getWindowHandles()) {
            if (!handle.equals(mainWindow)) {
                driver.switchTo().window(handle).close();
                break;
            }
        }
        driver.switchTo().window(mainWindow);
    }

    public void switchToOTPTab() { driver.findElement(otpTab).click(); }
    public void enterMobile(String mobile) { driver.findElement(mobileField).sendKeys(mobile); }
    public void clickSendOTP() { driver.findElement(sendOtpBtn).click(); }
    public void enterOTP(String otp) { driver.findElement(otpField).sendKeys(otp); }
    public void clickVerifyOTP() { driver.findElement(verifyOtpBtn).click(); }

    public String getErrorMessage() {
        return wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(errorMsg)).getText();
    }

    public String getInfoMessage() {
        return wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(infoMsg)).getText();
    }
}

Validation

  • Assert dashboard URL contains /dashboard
  • Verify welcome message text matches expected
  • Negative cases: error messages displayed, user stays on login page
  • SSO: window handle switch validated, popup closed on cancel
  • Screenshot captured on assertion failure via TestNG listener

Jira Workflow

StageJira StatusAction
RequirementTo DoCreate story QA-101: Multi-method Login Automation
DevelopmentIn ProgressBranch feature/QA-101-login-automation
Code ReviewPeer ReviewPR linked to QA-101, 2 approvals required
CI ExecutionTestingJenkins runs @smoke on merge; full suite nightly
Sign-offDoneAttach Cucumber HTML report + test evidence

Scenario 2: E-Commerce Checkout Flow

Requirement

Automate end-to-end checkout: browse products, add to cart, apply coupon, enter shipping, pay via card, and verify order confirmation. Use Scenario Outline for multiple products. Validate order in UI and MySQL database.

Feature File (Gherkin)

Feature: E-Commerce Checkout
  As a customer
  I want to purchase products online
  So that I receive order confirmation

  Background:
    Given I am logged in as "buyer@test.com"
    And the product catalog is available

  @checkout @smoke
  Scenario Outline: Purchase product with valid payment
    When I add product "" priced at $ to cart
    And I proceed to checkout
    And I enter shipping address "123 Main St, NY 10001"
    And I apply coupon code ""
    And I pay with card "4111111111111111" expiry "12/28" cvv "123"
    Then I should see order confirmation with total "$"
    And order should exist in database with status "CONFIRMED"

    Examples:
      | product      | price | coupon  | expectedTotal |
      | Laptop Pro   | 999   | SAVE10  | 899.10        |
      | Wireless Mouse| 29   | FLAT5   | 24.00         |
      | USB-C Hub    | 49    |         | 49.00         |
      | Monitor 27"  | 349   | SAVE10  | 314.10        |

  @checkout @negative
  Scenario: Checkout fails with declined card
    When I add product "Laptop Pro" priced at $999 to cart
    And I proceed to checkout
    And I enter shipping address "123 Main St, NY 10001"
    And I pay with card "4000000000000002" expiry "12/28" cvv "123"
    Then I should see payment error "Card declined"
    And order should NOT exist in database

Step Definition (Java)

package com.automation.steps;

import com.automation.pages.*;
import com.automation.utils.*;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.testng.Assert;
import java.sql.*;
import java.util.Map;

public class CheckoutSteps {
    private CatalogPage catalog;
    private CartPage cart;
    private CheckoutPage checkout;
    private ConfirmationPage confirmation;
    private String orderId;

    @Given("I am logged in as {string}")
    public void login(String email) {
        DriverFactory.getDriver().get("https://shop.example.com");
        new LoginPage(DriverFactory.getDriver()).login(email, "Pass@123");
    }

    @Given("the product catalog is available")
    public void openCatalog() {
        catalog = new CatalogPage(DriverFactory.getDriver());
        catalog.waitForProductsLoaded();
    }

    @When("I add product {string} priced at ${int} to cart")
    public void addToCart(String product, int price) {
        catalog.addProductToCart(product);
        cart = new CartPage(DriverFactory.getDriver());
        Assert.assertEquals(cart.getItemCount(), 1);
        Assert.assertTrue(cart.getSubtotal() >= price);
    }

    @When("I proceed to checkout")
    public void proceedCheckout() {
        cart.clickCheckout();
        checkout = new CheckoutPage(DriverFactory.getDriver());
    }

    @When("I enter shipping address {string}")
    public void enterAddress(String address) {
        checkout.fillShippingAddress(address);
    }

    @When("I apply coupon code {string}")
    public void applyCoupon(String coupon) {
        if (!coupon.isEmpty()) checkout.applyCoupon(coupon);
    }

    @When("I pay with card {string} expiry {string} cvv {string}")
    public void pay(String card, String expiry, String cvv) {
        checkout.enterPaymentDetails(card, expiry, cvv);
        checkout.clickPlaceOrder();
    }

    @Then("I should see order confirmation with total {string}")
    public void verifyConfirmation(String total) {
        confirmation = new ConfirmationPage(DriverFactory.getDriver());
        Assert.assertTrue(confirmation.isSuccessDisplayed());
        orderId = confirmation.getOrderId();
        Assert.assertEquals(confirmation.getOrderTotal(), total);
    }

    @Then("order should exist in database with status {string}")
    public void verifyDBOrder(String status) throws SQLException {
        Map<String, Object> row = DBUtil.querySingle(
            "SELECT status, total FROM orders WHERE order_id = ?", orderId);
        Assert.assertNotNull(row);
        Assert.assertEquals(row.get("status"), status);
    }

    @Then("I should see payment error {string}")
    public void verifyPaymentError(String error) {
        Assert.assertEquals(checkout.getPaymentError(), error);
    }

    @Then("order should NOT exist in database")
    public void verifyNoOrder() throws SQLException {
        Map<String, Object> row = DBUtil.querySingle(
            "SELECT order_id FROM orders WHERE user_email = ?", "buyer@test.com");
        Assert.assertNull(row);
    }
}

Page Object

package com.automation.pages;

import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.support.ui.*;

public class CheckoutPage {
    private WebDriver driver;
    private WebDriverWait wait;

    public CheckoutPage(WebDriver driver) {
        this.driver = driver;
        this.wait = new WebDriverWait(driver, Duration.ofSeconds(20));
    }

    public void fillShippingAddress(String address) {
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(By.id("address")));
        driver.findElement(By.id("address")).sendKeys(address);
        driver.findElement(By.id("continue-shipping")).click();
    }

    public void applyCoupon(String code) {
        driver.findElement(By.id("coupon")).sendKeys(code);
        driver.findElement(By.id("apply-coupon")).click();
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.textToBePresentInElementLocated(
            By.cssSelector(".discount-applied"), code));
    }

    public void enterPaymentDetails(String card, String expiry, String cvv) {
        wait.until(ExpectedConditions.frameToBeAvailableAndSwitchToIt(By.id("payment-frame")));
        driver.findElement(By.id("card-number")).sendKeys(card);
        driver.findElement(By.id("expiry")).sendKeys(expiry);
        driver.findElement(By.id("cvv")).sendKeys(cvv);
        driver.switchTo().defaultContent();
    }

    public void clickPlaceOrder() {
        driver.findElement(By.id("place-order")).click();
    }

    public String getPaymentError() {
        return wait.until(ExpectedConditions.visibilityOfElementLocated(
            By.cssSelector(".payment-error"))).getText();
    }
}

Validation

  • UI: cart count, subtotal, discount, final total on confirmation page
  • Database: SELECT status, total FROM orders WHERE order_id = ?
  • Negative: declined card shows error, no row inserted in orders table
  • Coupon math verified: price minus discount equals expectedTotal

QA-211Sub-taskScenario Outline for multi-product checkout
QA-212Sub-taskMySQL JDBC validation utility

Scenario 3: API Validation

Requirement

Implement REST Assured + Cucumber CRUD tests for User API. Cover POST create, GET verify, PUT update, DELETE cleanup. Validate status codes, response body, and response time.

Feature File (Gherkin)

Feature: User API CRUD Operations
  As an API consumer
  I want to manage users via REST endpoints
  So that user data is correctly persisted

  Background:
    Given the API base URL is "https://api.example.com"
    And the API key is configured

  @api @create
  Scenario: Create a new user via POST
    When I send POST request to "/users" with body:
      """
      {"name":"John Doe","email":"john@api.test","role":"member"}
      """
    Then the response status code should be 201
    And the response should contain field "id"
    And the response field "email" should be "john@api.test"
    And response time should be less than 2000 ms

  @api @read
  Scenario: Get user by ID via GET
    Given a user exists with email "jane@api.test"
    When I send GET request to "/users/{userId}"
    Then the response status code should be 200
    And the response field "name" should be "Jane Doe"

  @api @update
  Scenario: Update user via PUT
    Given a user exists with email "update@api.test"
    When I send PUT request to "/users/{userId}" with body:
      """
      {"name":"Updated Name","role":"admin"}
      """
    Then the response status code should be 200
    And the response field "name" should be "Updated Name"
    And the response field "role" should be "admin"

  @api @delete
  Scenario: Delete user via DELETE
    Given a user exists with email "delete@api.test"
    When I send DELETE request to "/users/{userId}"
    Then the response status code should be 204
    When I send GET request to "/users/{userId}"
    Then the response status code should be 404

  @api @negative
  Scenario: Create user with invalid email returns 400
    When I send POST request to "/users" with body:
      """
      {"name":"Bad Email","email":"not-an-email","role":"member"}
      """
    Then the response status code should be 400
    And the response should contain error message "Invalid email format"

Step Definition (Java)

package com.automation.api.steps;

import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import io.restassured.response.Response;
import io.restassured.specification.RequestSpecification;
import org.testng.Assert;
import static io.restassured.RestAssured.*;
import static org.hamcrest.Matchers.*;

public class UserApiSteps {
    private RequestSpecification request;
    private Response response;
    private String userId;
    private long startTime;

    @Given("the API base URL is {string}")
    public void setBaseUrl(String url) {
        baseURI = url;
        request = given().header("Content-Type", "application/json");
    }

    @Given("the API key is configured")
    public void setApiKey() {
        request = request.header("X-API-Key", System.getProperty("api.key", "test-key-123"));
    }

    @Given("a user exists with email {string}")
    public void createUser(String email) {
        response = request.body("{\"name\":\"Jane Doe\",\"email\":\"" + email + "\",\"role\":\"member\"}")
                          .post("/users");
        userId = response.jsonPath().getString("id");
    }

    @When("I send POST request to {string} with body:")
    public void postRequest(String endpoint, String body) {
        startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        response = request.body(body).post(endpoint);
    }

    @When("I send GET request to {string}")
    public void getRequest(String endpoint) {
        startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        String path = endpoint.replace("{userId}", userId);
        response = request.get(path);
    }

    @When("I send PUT request to {string} with body:")
    public void putRequest(String endpoint, String body) {
        String path = endpoint.replace("{userId}", userId);
        response = request.body(body).put(path);
    }

    @When("I send DELETE request to {string}")
    public void deleteRequest(String endpoint) {
        String path = endpoint.replace("{userId}", userId);
        response = request.delete(path);
    }

    @Then("the response status code should be {int}")
    public void verifyStatus(int code) {
        Assert.assertEquals(response.getStatusCode(), code);
    }

    @Then("the response should contain field {string}")
    public void verifyFieldExists(String field) {
        Assert.assertNotNull(response.jsonPath().get(field));
        userId = response.jsonPath().getString("id");
    }

    @Then("the response field {string} should be {string}")
    public void verifyFieldValue(String field, String expected) {
        Assert.assertEquals(response.jsonPath().getString(field), expected);
    }

    @Then("response time should be less than {int} ms")
    public void verifyResponseTime(int maxMs) {
        long elapsed = System.currentTimeMillis() - startTime;
        Assert.assertTrue(elapsed < maxMs, "Response took " + elapsed + "ms");
    }

    @Then("the response should contain error message {string}")
    public void verifyErrorMessage(String msg) {
        Assert.assertTrue(response.jsonPath().getString("error").contains(msg));
    }
}

Page Object

API tests use a Service Object pattern instead of Page Objects:

package com.automation.api.services;

import io.restassured.response.Response;
import static io.restassured.RestAssured.*;

public class UserApiService {
    public Response createUser(String name, String email, String role) {
        return given().header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                      .body("{\"name\":\"" + name + "\",\"email\":\"" + email + "\",\"role\":\"" + role + "\"}")
                      .post("/users");
    }

    public Response getUser(String userId) {
        return given().get("/users/" + userId);
    }

    public Response updateUser(String userId, String body) {
        return given().header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                      .body(body).put("/users/" + userId);
    }

    public Response deleteUser(String userId) {
        return given().delete("/users/" + userId);
    }
}

Validation

  • Status codes: 201 (create), 200 (read/update), 204 (delete), 404 (not found), 400 (bad request)
  • JSON path assertions on id, name, email, role fields
  • Response time SLA under 2000ms
  • DELETE followed by GET confirms resource removal

TestingRun @api tag in CI pipeline post-deploy to staging
DoneAllure report attached; contract tests pass against OpenAPI spec

Scenario 4: Database Validation

Requirement

Verify UI-displayed employee data matches MySQL database records. Use JDBC in step definitions. Cover insert-via-UI-then-verify-DB and seed-DB-then-verify-UI flows for data integrity.

Feature File (Gherkin)

Feature: Database Data Integrity Validation
  As a QA engineer
  I want to verify UI data matches the database
  So that data integrity is maintained

  Background:
    Given database connection is established
    And I am on the employee management page

  @db @smoke
  Scenario: UI employee list matches database records
    When I fetch all employees from UI
    Then UI employee count should match database count
    And each UI employee should match database record

  @db
  Scenario: New employee created in UI appears in database
    When I create employee with name "Alice Smith" department "Engineering" salary "85000"
    Then employee "Alice Smith" should exist in database
    And database field "department" for "Alice Smith" should be "Engineering"
    And database field "salary" for "Alice Smith" should be "85000"

  @db
  Scenario: Employee updated in UI reflects in database
    Given employee "Bob Jones" exists in database with department "Sales"
    When I update employee "Bob Jones" department to "Marketing"
    Then database field "department" for "Bob Jones" should be "Marketing"

  @db @negative
  Scenario: Deleted employee removed from database
    Given employee "Temp User" exists in database
    When I delete employee "Temp User" from UI
    Then employee "Temp User" should NOT exist in database

Step Definition (Java)

package com.automation.steps;

import com.automation.pages.EmployeePage;
import com.automation.utils.*;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.testng.Assert;
import java.sql.*;
import java.util.*;

public class DatabaseValidationSteps {
    private Connection conn;
    private EmployeePage empPage;
    private List<Map<String, String>> uiEmployees;

    @Given("database connection is established")
    public void connectDB() throws SQLException {
        conn = DBUtil.getConnection(
            ConfigReader.get("db.url"),
            ConfigReader.get("db.user"),
            ConfigReader.get("db.password"));
        Assert.assertFalse(conn.isClosed());
    }

    @Given("I am on the employee management page")
    public void openEmployeePage() {
        DriverFactory.getDriver().get(ConfigReader.get("app.url") + "/employees");
        empPage = new EmployeePage(DriverFactory.getDriver());
    }

    @When("I fetch all employees from UI")
    public void fetchUIEmployees() {
        uiEmployees = empPage.getAllEmployees();
    }

    @Then("UI employee count should match database count")
    public void compareCount() throws SQLException {
        int dbCount = DBUtil.queryCount(conn, "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM employees WHERE active = 1");
        Assert.assertEquals(uiEmployees.size(), dbCount);
    }

    @Then("each UI employee should match database record")
    public void compareRecords() throws SQLException {
        for (Map<String, String> uiEmp : uiEmployees) {
            Map<String, Object> dbRow = DBUtil.querySingle(conn,
                "SELECT name, department, salary FROM employees WHERE id = ?",
                uiEmp.get("id"));
            Assert.assertEquals(uiEmp.get("name"), dbRow.get("name"));
            Assert.assertEquals(uiEmp.get("department"), dbRow.get("department"));
        }
    }

    @When("I create employee with name {string} department {string} salary {string}")
    public void createEmployee(String name, String dept, String salary) {
        empPage.clickAddEmployee();
        empPage.fillEmployeeForm(name, dept, salary);
        empPage.saveEmployee();
    }

    @Then("employee {string} should exist in database")
    public void verifyExists(String name) throws SQLException {
        Map<String, Object> row = DBUtil.querySingle(conn,
            "SELECT id FROM employees WHERE name = ?", name);
        Assert.assertNotNull(row, "Employee not found in DB: " + name);
    }

    @Then("database field {string} for {string} should be {string}")
    public void verifyDBField(String field, String name, String expected) throws SQLException {
        Map<String, Object> row = DBUtil.querySingle(conn,
            "SELECT " + field + " FROM employees WHERE name = ?", name);
        Assert.assertEquals(String.valueOf(row.get(field)), expected);
    }

    @Given("employee {string} exists in database with department {string}")
    public void seedEmployee(String name, String dept) throws SQLException {
        DBUtil.execute(conn,
            "INSERT INTO employees (name, department, salary, active) VALUES (?, ?, 60000, 1)",
            name, dept);
        empPage.refreshPage();
    }

    @When("I update employee {string} department to {string}")
    public void updateEmployee(String name, String dept) {
        empPage.editEmployee(name);
        empPage.setDepartment(dept);
        empPage.saveEmployee();
    }

    @When("I delete employee {string} from UI")
    public void deleteEmployee(String name) {
        empPage.deleteEmployee(name);
        empPage.confirmDelete();
    }

    @Then("employee {string} should NOT exist in database")
    public void verifyNotExists(String name) throws SQLException {
        Map<String, Object> row = DBUtil.querySingle(conn,
            "SELECT id FROM employees WHERE name = ?", name);
        Assert.assertNull(row);
    }
}

Page Object

package com.automation.pages;

import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import java.util.*;

public class EmployeePage {
    private WebDriver driver;

    public EmployeePage(WebDriver driver) { this.driver = driver; }

    public List<Map<String, String>> getAllEmployees() {
        List<Map<String, String>> list = new ArrayList<>();
        List<WebElement> rows = driver.findElements(By.cssSelector("#employee-table tbody tr"));
        for (WebElement row : rows) {
            Map<String, String> emp = new HashMap<>();
            emp.put("id", row.findElement(By.cssSelector("[data-field='id']")).getText());
            emp.put("name", row.findElement(By.cssSelector("[data-field='name']")).getText());
            emp.put("department", row.findElement(By.cssSelector("[data-field='dept']")).getText());
            list.add(emp);
        }
        return list;
    }

    public void clickAddEmployee() { driver.findElement(By.id("add-employee")).click(); }
    public void fillEmployeeForm(String name, String dept, String salary) {
        driver.findElement(By.id("emp-name")).sendKeys(name);
        driver.findElement(By.id("emp-dept")).sendKeys(dept);
        driver.findElement(By.id("emp-salary")).sendKeys(salary);
    }
    public void saveEmployee() { driver.findElement(By.id("save-employee")).click(); }
    public void refreshPage() { driver.navigate().refresh(); }
    public void editEmployee(String name) {
        driver.findElement(By.xpath("//tr[td='" + name + "']//button[@data-action='edit']")).click();
    }
    public void setDepartment(String dept) {
        driver.findElement(By.id("emp-dept")).clear();
        driver.findElement(By.id("emp-dept")).sendKeys(dept);
    }
    public void deleteEmployee(String name) {
        driver.findElement(By.xpath("//tr[td='" + name + "']//button[@data-action='delete']")).click();
    }
    public void confirmDelete() { driver.findElement(By.id("confirm-delete")).click(); }
}

Validation

  • Row count: UI table rows == SELECT COUNT(*) FROM employees WHERE active=1
  • Field-level match: name, department, salary compared per record
  • Insert flow: UI create → DB SELECT confirms new row
  • Update flow: UI edit → DB field value updated
  • Delete flow: UI delete → DB row absent or active=0

QA-402MediumTest data seeding scripts for preconditions
QA-403LowConnection pooling optimization for parallel runs

Scenario 5: Cross-Browser Execution

Requirement

Execute the same Cucumber scenarios in parallel across Chrome and Firefox using TestNG suite XML. Use ConfigReader for browser selection, tag-based filtering (@chrome, @firefox), and compare execution results across browsers.

Feature File (Gherkin)

Feature: Cross-Browser Compatibility
  As a QA team
  I want to run tests on multiple browsers
  So that the application works consistently

  @crossbrowser @chrome @smoke
  Scenario: Homepage loads correctly in Chrome
    Given I open the application homepage
    Then the page title should be "Example App"
    And the navigation menu should be visible
    And the login button should be clickable

  @crossbrowser @firefox @smoke
  Scenario: Homepage loads correctly in Firefox
    Given I open the application homepage
    Then the page title should be "Example App"
    And the navigation menu should be visible
    And the login button should be clickable

  @crossbrowser @chrome
  Scenario: Search functionality works in Chrome
    Given I open the application homepage
    When I search for "automation testing"
    Then search results should contain "automation testing"

  @crossbrowser @firefox
  Scenario: Search functionality works in Firefox
    Given I open the application homepage
    When I search for "automation testing"
    Then search results should contain "automation testing"

  @crossbrowser @chrome @firefox
  Scenario: Contact form submission
    Given I open the application homepage
    When I fill contact form with name "Test User" email "test@cb.com"
    And I submit the contact form
    Then I should see success message "Thank you for contacting us"

Step Definition (Java)

package com.automation.steps;

import com.automation.utils.*;
import io.cucumber.java.en.*;
import org.openqa.selenium.*;
import org.testng.Assert;

public class CrossBrowserSteps {
    private WebDriver driver;

    @Given("I open the application homepage")
    public void openHomepage() {
        driver = DriverFactory.getDriver();
        driver.get(ConfigReader.get("app.url"));
    }

    @Then("the page title should be {string}")
    public void verifyTitle(String title) {
        Assert.assertEquals(driver.getTitle(), title);
    }

    @Then("the navigation menu should be visible")
    public void verifyNavMenu() {
        WebElement nav = driver.findElement(By.id("main-nav"));
        Assert.assertTrue(nav.isDisplayed());
    }

    @Then("the login button should be clickable")
    public void verifyLoginButton() {
        WebElement btn = driver.findElement(By.id("login-btn"));
        Assert.assertTrue(btn.isEnabled());
    }

    @When("I search for {string}")
    public void search(String term) {
        driver.findElement(By.id("search-input")).sendKeys(term);
        driver.findElement(By.id("search-btn")).click();
    }

    @Then("search results should contain {string}")
    public void verifySearchResults(String term) {
        WebElement results = driver.findElement(By.id("search-results"));
        Assert.assertTrue(results.getText().toLowerCase().contains(term.toLowerCase()));
    }

    @When("I fill contact form with name {string} email {string}")
    public void fillContactForm(String name, String email) {
        driver.findElement(By.id("contact-name")).sendKeys(name);
        driver.findElement(By.id("contact-email")).sendKeys(email);
        driver.findElement(By.id("contact-message")).sendKeys("Cross-browser test message");
    }

    @When("I submit the contact form")
    public void submitContactForm() {
        driver.findElement(By.id("contact-submit")).click();
    }

    @Then("I should see success message {string}")
    public void verifySuccess(String msg) {
        WebElement success = driver.findElement(By.cssSelector(".success-message"));
        Assert.assertEquals(success.getText(), msg);
    }
}

Page Object & Config

// ConfigReader.java
package com.automation.utils;

import java.io.*;
import java.util.Properties;

public class ConfigReader {
    private static Properties props = new Properties();
    static {
        try (InputStream is = ConfigReader.class.getClassLoader()
                .getResourceAsStream("config.properties")) {
            props.load(is);
        } catch (IOException e) { throw new RuntimeException(e); }
    }
    public static String get(String key) {
        String sysVal = System.getProperty(key);
        return sysVal != null ? sysVal : props.getProperty(key);
    }
    public static String getBrowser() {
        return get("browser"); // set via -Dbrowser=chrome or testng parameter
    }
}

// DriverFactory.java — browser selected from ConfigReader
public class DriverFactory {
    private static ThreadLocal<WebDriver> tlDriver = new ThreadLocal<>();

    public static WebDriver getDriver() {
        if (tlDriver.get() == null) {
            String browser = ConfigReader.getBrowser();
            switch (browser.toLowerCase()) {
                case "firefox":
                    tlDriver.set(new FirefoxDriver());
                    break;
                default:
                    tlDriver.set(new ChromeDriver());
            }
            tlDriver.get().manage().window().maximize();
        }
        return tlDriver.get();
    }

    public static void quitDriver() {
        if (tlDriver.get() != null) {
            tlDriver.get().quit();
            tlDriver.remove();
        }
    }
}

testng.xml — Parallel Browsers

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE suite SYSTEM "https://testng.org/testng-1.0.dtd">
<suite name="Cross-Browser Suite" parallel="tests" thread-count="2" verbose="1">

  <parameter name="browser" value="chrome"/>
  <test name="Chrome Tests">
    <parameter name="cucumber.filter.tags" value="@chrome"/>
    <classes>
      <class name="com.automation.runners.ChromeTestRunner"/>
    </classes>
  </test>

  <parameter name="browser" value="firefox"/>
  <test name="Firefox Tests">
    <parameter name="cucumber.filter.tags" value="@firefox"/>
    <classes>
      <class name="com.automation.runners.FirefoxTestRunner"/>
    </classes>
  </test>

</suite>

Validation & Results Comparison

  • Each browser test produces separate Cucumber JSON report: target/cucumber-reports/chrome/report.json
  • Compare pass/fail counts across browsers using a post-run script
  • Flag browser-specific failures (e.g., CSS rendering, JS compatibility)
  • Screenshot diff optional for visual regression

Section 31: TestNG Cheat Sheet

Annotations

AnnotationPurposeExecution Order
@BeforeSuiteRuns once before all tests in suite1 (earliest)
@BeforeTestRuns before each <test> tag in XML2
@BeforeClassRuns once before first method in class3
@BeforeMethodRuns before each @Test method4
@TestMarks a test method5
@AfterMethodRuns after each @Test method6
@AfterClassRuns once after all methods in class7
@AfterTestRuns after each <test> tag in XML8
@AfterSuiteRuns once after all tests in suite9 (latest)
@BeforeGroupsRuns before first method in specified groupsBefore @Test in group
@AfterGroupsRuns after last method in specified groupsAfter @Test in group
@DataProviderSupplies data to test methodsBefore @Test invocation
@FactoryCreates test class instances dynamicallyDuring suite init
@ParametersPasses parameters from testng.xmlBefore @Test invocation

Assertions

MethodDescriptionExample
assertEquals(actual, expected)Checks equalityAssert.assertEquals(result, 200);
assertNotEquals(a, b)Checks inequalityAssert.assertNotEquals(status, "FAIL");
assertTrue(condition)Condition must be trueAssert.assertTrue(driver.findElement(btn).isDisplayed());
assertFalse(condition)Condition must be falseAssert.assertFalse(list.isEmpty());
assertNull(object)Object must be nullAssert.assertNull(errorMsg);
assertNotNull(object)Object must not be nullAssert.assertNotNull(userId);
assertSame(a, b)Same reference (==)Assert.assertSame(driver1, driver1);
assertNotSame(a, b)Different referencesAssert.assertNotSame(obj1, obj2);
fail(message)Force test failureAssert.fail("Unexpected state");
SoftAssertCollect failures, assertAll() at endSoftAssert s = new SoftAssert(); s.assertAll();

@Test Attributes

AttributeTypeDefaultDescription
priorityint0Lower value runs first among methods in same class
groupsString[]{}Assign test to groups for include/exclude
dependsOnMethodsString[]{}Run only if dependent methods pass
dependsOnGroupsString[]{}Depends on all methods in specified groups
enabledbooleantrueSet false to skip test
timeOutlong (ms)0Max execution time before failure
invocationCountint1Number of times to invoke test
threadPoolSizeint0Pool size when invocationCount > 1
dataProviderString""Name of data provider method
expectedExceptionsClass[]{}Test passes if listed exception thrown
retryAnalyzerClassnoneCustom retry logic on failure
descriptionString""Human-readable test description

Groups — XML Include/Exclude

<!DOCTYPE suite SYSTEM "https://testng.org/testng-1.0.dtd">
<suite name="Group Suite">
  <test name="Smoke Only">
    <groups>
      <run>
        <include name="smoke"/>
        <exclude name="broken"/>
      </run>
    </groups>
    <classes>
      <class name="com.tests.LoginTest"/>
    </classes>
  </test>
</suite>

// In Java:
@Test(groups = {"smoke", "regression"})
public void testLogin() { }

DataProvider Template

@DataProvider(name = "loginData")
public Object[][] getLoginData() {
    return new Object[][] {
        {"user1@test.com", "pass1", true},
        {"bad@test.com",   "wrong", false},
        {"",               "pass",  false}
    };
}

@Test(dataProvider = "loginData")
public void testLogin(String email, String pass, boolean expected) {
    boolean result = loginPage.login(email, pass);
    Assert.assertEquals(result, expected);
}

// Parallel data provider:
@DataProvider(name = "data", parallel = true)
public Object[][] parallelData() {
    return new Object[][] { {1}, {2}, {3} };
}

Listeners

InterfaceKey MethodsUse Case

RetryAnalyzer Template

public class RetryAnalyzer implements IRetryAnalyzer {
    private int count = 0;
    private static final int MAX_RETRY = 2;

    @Override
    public boolean retry(ITestResult result) {
        if (count < MAX_RETRY) {
            count++;
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

// Usage:
@Test(retryAnalyzer = RetryAnalyzer.class)
public void flakyTest() { }

// Global retry via IAnnotationTransformer:
public class AnnotationTransformer implements IAnnotationTransformer {
    public void transform(Annotation annotation, Class testClass,
                          Constructor ctor, Method method) {
        if (annotation instanceof Test) {
            ((Test) annotation).setRetryAnalyzer(RetryAnalyzer.class);
        }
    }
}

Parallel Modes

ModeWhat Runs Parallelthread-count
parallel="tests"Each <test> tag in parallelNumber of concurrent tests
parallel="classes"Test classes within a <test>Number of concurrent classes
parallel="methods"@Test methods within a classNumber of concurrent methods
parallel="instances"Test class instances (@Factory)Number of concurrent instances
DataProvider parallel=trueData provider iterationsUses suite thread-count

Complete testng.xml Template

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE suite SYSTEM "https://testng.org/testng-1.0.dtd">
<suite name="Automation Suite" parallel="methods" thread-count="4" verbose="2">

  <listeners>
    <listener class-name="com.listeners.TestListener"/>
    <listener class-name="com.listeners.ReportListener"/>
  </listeners>

  <parameter name="browser" value="chrome"/>
  <parameter name="env" value="staging"/>

  <test name="Regression Tests">
    <groups>
      <run>
        <include name="regression"/>
        <exclude name="wip"/>
      </run>
    </groups>
    <packages>
      <package name="com.tests.ui"/>
    </packages>
  </test>

  <test name="API Tests">
    <classes>
      <class name="com.tests.api.UserApiTest"/>
    </classes>
  </test>

</suite>

mvn test -Dgroups=smokeRun tests in smoke group
mvn test -Dtest=LoginTestRun single test class
mvn test -Dtest=LoginTest#testValidLoginRun single test method
mvn test -Dparallel=methods -DthreadCount=5Override parallel settings
mvn clean test -Dsurefire.rerunFailingTestsCount=2Auto-retry failed tests

Quick Tip: Configure surefire plugin in pom.xml with <suiteXmlFiles>testng.xml</suiteXmlFiles> to run TestNG by default on mvn test.

Section 33: Interview Preparation

350 questions with Answer and Interviewer Expects. Format: every entry includes a concise 3–5 line answer and what the interviewer is evaluating.

Top 100 TestNG Questions

Basic (30)

Q1: What is TestNG and why use it over JUnit?

Answer: TestNG (Test Next Generation) is a Java testing framework inspired by JUnit and NUnit. It provides advanced features like parallel execution, data providers, grouping, dependency testing, and flexible XML-based suite configuration. TestNG supports annotations for fine-grained lifecycle control (@BeforeSuite through @AfterMethod). It integrates seamlessly with Selenium, Maven, and CI/CD pipelines. Reporting is richer with default HTML reports and listener extensibility.

Interviewer expects: Clear comparison showing you chose TestNG for enterprise automation needs, not just naming features.

Q2: What annotations does TestNG provide for test lifecycle?

Answer: TestNG provides @BeforeSuite, @AfterSuite, @BeforeTest, @AfterTest, @BeforeClass, @AfterClass, @BeforeMethod, @AfterMethod, and @BeforeGroups/@AfterGroups. @BeforeSuite runs once before all tests; @BeforeMethod runs before each @Test. Execution order: Suite → Test → Class → Method. These annotations replace setup/teardown boilerplate and enable layered test initialization for UI, API, and DB layers independently.

Interviewer expects: Correct execution order and knowing which annotation runs at which scope.

Q3: What is the execution order of TestNG annotations?

Answer: Order: @BeforeSuite → @BeforeTest → @BeforeClass → @BeforeMethod → @Test → @AfterMethod → @AfterClass → @AfterTest → @AfterSuite. @BeforeGroups runs before the first method in matching groups; @AfterGroups runs after the last. Multiple @Test methods in a class each trigger @BeforeMethod/@AfterMethod pair. Priority attribute affects @Test order within a class but not lifecycle annotations.

Interviewer expects: Precise ordering without confusing @BeforeTest with @BeforeMethod scope.

Q4: How do you create a basic TestNG test?

Answer: Create a Java class, import org.testng.annotations.Test and org.testng.Assert. Annotate test methods with @Test. Use Assert.assertEquals, assertTrue, etc. for validations.
